**[23:45:29] 🟥用户**

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   - Redesign `/db` command to show real database statistics (file size, table count, row counts per table grouped by subsystem) instead of memory tags
   - Make `/db` output professional and polished for imminent release
   - Every table group must have accurate names from actual source code — no generic "其他" allowed
   - Redesign `/memory` command with better formatting (source distribution, relative time, importance indicator)
   - Rename `/users` to `/user-memories` — no backward compatibility tolerated
   - Add `/relationship` command to show relationship data per user
   - Improve `/intent` command to show more than just pending intent
   - Add `/learn` command to show learning status (queue + learned procedures)
   - User identity is 陈丽君

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - All memory subsystems share one SQLite file: `~/.xiaomei-brain/{agent_id}/memory/brain.db`
   - `SQLiteStore` is the shared base class with lazy connection, WAL journal, `db_path` property
   - Color scheme: Green `\033[32m` (primary), Coral `\033[38;5;203m` (values), Teal `\033[38;5;73m` (labels), Gray `\033[90m` (hints/metadata)
   - Unified command dispatch: Gateway `_dispatch_command()` → 3-tier (data/special/system)
   - `_DATA_CMDS` frozenset in `inbound.py` controls which commands route to `MemoryConsole.execute()`
   - Table groups based on owning classes from code: ConversationDB, DAGSummaryGraph, LongTermMemory, ExperienceStream, PurposeStorage, GoalRunStorage, ProcedureMemory, TaskQueueStorage, RelationshipEngine, Essence, ProjectMentalModel, AgentInbox
   - FTS5 internal tables (`_fts`, `_fts_config`, `_fts_data`, `_fts_docsize`, `_fts_idx`) filtered from display
   - Thousand separators: `{cnt:,}`, relative time: `3h前`/`23d前`, importance: ▮(≥0.7)/▯(≥0.4)/·(<0.4)

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/agent/commands.py`** (heaviest changes)
     - Added `import os` at top
     - `_cmd_db()` — complete rewrite showing db path, size, table groups with row counts
     - `_cmd_memory()` — complete rewrite with header, source distribution, relative time, importance
     - `_cmd_users()` — redesign with "用户记忆分布" header, aligned columns, percentages
     - `_cmd_relationship()` — new command for user relationship data
     - `_cmd_learn()` — new command for learning queue + procedures
     - Command routing: `user-memories` → `_cmd_users()`, `relationship` → `_cmd_relationship()`, `learn` → `_cmd_learn()`
     - Help text updated for all new/changed commands
     
     Final `_cmd_db()`:
     ```python
     def _cmd_db(self, user_id: str) -> CommandResult:
         """Database statistics — size, tables, row counts."""
         lines: list[str] = []
         data: dict[str, Any] = {}
         G, V, D, X, R = "\033[32m", "\033[38;5;203m", "\033[38;5;73m", "\033[90m", "\033[0m"

         db_source = self.db or self.dag or self.ltm
         if not db_source:
             return CommandResult(output=f"  {D}(无数据库){R}")

         db_path = str(db_source.db_path)
         db_name = os.path.basename(db_path)
         home = os.path.expanduser("~")
         display_path = "~" + db_path[len(home):] if db_path.startswith(home) else db_path

         size_str = "N/A"
         try:
             size_bytes = os.path.getsize(db_path)
             if size_bytes >= 1024 * 1024:
                 size_str = f"{size_bytes / (1024 * 1024):.1f} MB"
             elif size_bytes >= 1024:
                 size_str = f"{size_bytes / 1024:.1f} KB"
             else:
                 size_str = f"{size_bytes} B"
             data["size_bytes"] = size_bytes
         except OSError:
             size_bytes = 0

         lines.append(f"  {G}数据库{R}  {db_name}")
         lines.append(f"  {D}路径{R}    {display_path}")

         conn = db_source._get_conn()
         tables = conn.execute(
             "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master "
             "WHERE type='table' AND name NOT LIKE 'sqlite_%' AND name != 'schema_versions' "
             "ORDER BY name"
         ).fetchall()

         total_rows = 0
         row_map: dict[str, int] = {}
         _fts_suffix = frozenset({"_fts", "_fts_config", "_fts_data", "_fts_docsize", "_fts_idx", "_fts_content"})
         for (tname,) in tables:
             if any(tname.endswith(s) for s in _fts_suffix):
                 continue
             try:
                 cnt = conn.execute(f"SELECT COUNT(*) FROM [{tname}]").fetchone()[0]
             except Exception:
                 cnt = 0
             total_rows += cnt
             row_map[tname] = cnt

         lines.append(f"  {D}大小{R}    {V}{size_str}{R}  {X}·{R}  {V}{len(tables)}{R} 张表  {X}·{R}  {V}{total_rows:,}{R} 行")

         groups: list[tuple[str, list[str]]] = [
             ("对话",          ["messages", "tool_history"]),
             ("DAG",           ["summaries"]),
             ("长期记忆",      ["memories", "memory_tags", "memory_history",
                               "memory_relations", "memory_co_occurrence",
                               "thoughts", "consciousness_stream", "narrative_memories"]),
             ("经验流",        ["experience_stream"]),
             ("Purpose",       ["goals"]),
             ("PACE",          ["goal_runs", "goal_steps", "goal_log", "pace_checkpoints"]),
             ("程序记忆",      ["procedure_memories"]),
             ("意识队列",      ["intent_buffer", "learning_queue"]),
             ("关系",          ["relationships"]),
             ("底色",          ["essence"]),
             ("项目认知",      ["project_map"]),
             ("Agent 通讯",    ["agent_inbox"]),
         ]

         grouped = set()
         for _, names in groups:
             grouped.update(names)
         other = [(n, row_map[n]) for n in sorted(row_map) if n not in grouped]

         col_w = max((len(n) for n in row_map), default=0) + 4

         for group_name, table_names in groups:
             present = [(n, row_map[n]) for n in table_names if n in row_map]
             if not present:
                 continue
             lines.append(f"\n  {G}{group_name}{R}")
             for tname, cnt in present:
                 lines.append(f"  {X}{tname:<{col_w}}{R}{V}{cnt:>8,}{R}")

         if other:
             lines.append(f"\n  {G}其他{R}")
             for tname, cnt in other:
                 lines.append(f"  {X}{tname:<{col_w}}{R}{V}{cnt:>8,}{R}")

         return CommandResult(output="\n".join(lines), data=data)
     ```

     Final `_cmd_memory()`:
     ```python
     def _cmd_memory(self, user_id: str) -> CommandResult:
         """List recent long-term memories."""
         import time as _time
         G, V, D, X, R = "\033[32m", "\033[38;5;203m", "\033[38;5;73m", "\033[90m", "\033[0m"
         if not self.ltm:
             return CommandResult(output=f"  {D}长期记忆未配置{R}")
         total = self.ltm.count(user_id=user_id)
         rows = self.ltm.get_recent(10, user_id=user_id)
         now = _time.time()
         conn = self.ltm._get_conn()
         src_rows = conn.execute(
             "SELECT source, COUNT(*) FROM memories WHERE user_id=? GROUP BY source ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC",
             (user_id,),
         ).fetchall()
         lines = [f"  {G}长期记忆{R}  {D}{user_id}{R}: {V}{total}{R} 条"]
         if src_rows:
             src_parts = [f"{X}{s}{R} {V}{c}{R}" for s, c in src_rows]
             lines.append(f"  {X}{' · '.join(src_parts)}{R}")
         if not rows:
             return CommandResult(output="\n".join(lines), data={"total": total, "memories": []})
         lines.append("")
         for i, r in enumerate(rows, 1):
             age = now - r["created_at"]
             if age < 3600:
                 ago = f"{int(age // 60)}m"
             elif age < 86400:
                 ago = f"{int(age // 3600)}h"
             else:
                 ago = f"{int(age // 86400)}d"
             content = r["content"][:80].replace("\n", " ")
             importance = r.get("importance", 0.5)
             imp_bar = "▮" if importance >= 0.7 else ("▯" if importance >= 0.4 else "·")
             lines.append(f"  {X}{i}.{R} {D}{r['source']:<10}{R} {content}")
             lines.append(f"     {X}{ago}前{R}  {G}{imp_bar}{R} {importance:.2f}")
         return CommandResult(
             output="\n".join(lines),
             data={"total": total, "memories": rows, "sources": {s: c for s, c in src_rows}},
         )
     ```

     Final `_cmd_users()`:
     ```python
     def _cmd_users(self) -> CommandResult:
         """Show memory counts per user."""
         G, V, D, X, R = "\033[32m", "\033[38;5;203m", "\033[38;5;73m", "\033[90m", "\033[0m"
         if not self.ltm:
             return CommandResult(output=f"  {D}LongTermMemory 未配置{R}")
         conn = self.ltm._get_conn()
         rows = conn.execute(
             "SELECT user_id, COUNT(*) FROM memories GROUP BY user_id ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC"
         ).fetchall()
         if not rows:
             return CommandResult(output=f"  {D}无用户记忆{R}")
         total = sum(r[1] for r in rows)
         max_id_len = max(len(r[0]) for r in rows)
         max_cnt_len = max(len(f"{r[1]:,}") for r in rows)
         lines = [f"  {G}用户记忆分布{R}  {V}{len(rows)}{R} 位用户, {V}{total:,}{R} 条"]
         for user_id, cnt in rows:
             pct = cnt / total * 100 if total else 0
             bar_w = max(1, int(pct / 5))
             bar = "█" * bar_w
             id_pad = " " * (max_id_len - len(user_id))
             cnt_pad = " " * (max_cnt_len - len(f"{cnt:,}"))
             lines.append(f"  {D}{user_id}{R}{id_pad}  {V}{cnt_pad}{cnt:,}{R}  {X}{bar}{R} {pct:.0f}%")
         return CommandResult(
             output="\n".join(lines),
             data={r[0]: r[1] for r in rows},
         )
     ```

     Final `_cmd_learn()` (new):
     ```python
     def _cmd_learn(self) -> CommandResult:
         """Show learning status — queue + learned procedures."""
         G, V, D, X, R = "\033[32m", "\033[38;5;203m", "\033[38;5;73m", "\033[90m", "\033[0m"
         db_source = self.db or self.dag or self.ltm
         if not db_source:
             return CommandResult(output=f"  {D}无数据库{R}")
         conn = db_source._get_conn()
         queue = conn.execute(
             "SELECT topic, reason, priority, source, status, created_at FROM learning_queue ORDER BY created_at DESC"
         ).fetchall()
         procs = conn.execute(
             "SELECT name, description, execution_count, execution_success_rate, weight, status FROM procedure_memories WHERE status != 'archived' ORDER BY weight DESC"
         ).fetchall()
         lines = [f"  {G}学习情况{R}"]
         lines.append(f"\n  {G}待学队列{R}  {V}{len(queue)}{R} 个主题")
         if queue:
             for q in queue:
                 status_mark = f"{G}→{R}" if q["status"] == "pending" else f"{X}✓{R}"
                 lines.append(f"  {status_mark} {D}{q['topic']}{R}  {X}priority={q['priority']:.2f}{R}")
                 if q["reason"]:
                     lines.append(f"    {X}{q['reason'][:80]}{R}")
         else:
             lines.append(f"  {X}暂无待学主题{R}")
         lines.append(f"\n  {G}已学程序{R}  {V}{len(procs)}{R} 个")
         if procs:
             for p in procs[:10]:
                 success = f"{p['execution_success_rate']:.1%}" if p['execution_count'] > 0 else "-"
                 lines.append(f"  {G}●{R} {p['name']}  {X}执行{p['execution_count']}次 成功率{success}  weight={p['weight']:.2f}{R}")
         else:
             lines.append(f"  {X}暂无{R}")
         return CommandResult(
             output="\n".join(lines),
             data={"queue": len(queue), "procedures": len(procs)},
         )
     ```

     ```python
     def cmd_show_intent(living: ConsciousLiving, args: str = "") -> None:
         """显示当前 Intent"""
         import time as _time
         logger.info("[CLI] 执行命令: intent")
         G, V, D, X, R = "\033[32m", "\033[38;5;203m", "\033[38;5;73m", "\033[90m", "\033[0m"
         now = _time.time()
         intent = living.consciousness.get_pending_intent()
         db_source = getattr(living.agent, 'conversation_db', None) or getattr(living.agent, 'longterm_memory', None)
         buf_total = buf_pending = buf_done = 0
         buf_recent: list = []
         if db_source:
             try:
                 conn = db_source._get_conn()
                 buf_total = conn.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM intent_buffer").fetchone()[0]
                 if buf_total > 0:
                     buf_pending = conn.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM intent_buffer WHERE status='pending'").fetchone()[0]
                     buf_done = conn.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM intent_buffer WHERE status='done'").fetchone()[0]
                     buf_recent = conn.execute(
                         "SELECT type, content, priority, status, created_at FROM intent_buffer ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 5"
                     ).fetchall()
             except Exception:
                 pass
         print(f"\n  {G}意图{R}", flush=True)
         if intent:
             print(f"  {D}待处理{R}  {V}{intent.type.value}{R}  priority={intent.priority:.2f}", flush=True)
             print(f"  {intent.content[:120]}", flush=True)
         else:
             print(f"  {D}待处理{R}  {X}无{R}", flush=True)
         if buf_total > 0:
             print(f"  {D}缓冲区{R}  {V}{buf_total}{R} 条  {X}(pending {buf_pending}, done {buf_done}){R}", flush=True)
             print(f"  {D}最近{R}", flush=True)
             for b in buf_recent:
                 ago = now - b["created_at"]
                 if ago < 3600:
                     ts = f"{int(ago // 60)}m前"
                 elif ago < 86400:
                     ts = f"{int(ago // 3600)}h前"
                 else:
                     ts = f"{int(ago // 86400)}d前"
                 status_mark = f"{G}●{R}" if b["status"] == "pending" else f"{X}○{R}"
                 print(f"  {status_mark} {D}{b['type']:<8}{R} {b['content'][:60]}  {X}{ts}{R}", flush=True)
         else:
             print(f"  {D}缓冲区{R}  {X}空{R}", flush=True)
         living._print_prompt()
     ```

**[23:46:28] 🤖助手**

基于对现有架构的了解，以下是我认为还可以增加的命令：

**数据查看类**

- `/self` — 查看当前 SelfImage（身份、追求、热爱、底线、生长记录）。这是意识系统的核心骨架，目前没有直接查看的命令
- `/essence` — 查看底色（性格基线），从 essence 表读取，了解 agent 的行为倾向
- `/stream` — 查看最近经验流（experience_stream 表），了解 agent "经历了什么"
- `/projects` — 查看项目心智模型（project_map 表），agent 对当前项目的理解

**系统运维类**

- `/sessions` — 列出最近会话（session 列表、消息数、时间），比 `/context` 更宏观
- `/procedures` — 查看程序记忆详情（参数签名、执行历史），比 `/learn` 中的简略展示更详细
- `/inbox` — 查看 Agent 间通讯收件箱（agent_inbox 表），P2P 消息

**统计概览类**

- `/stats` — 全局统计面板（对话总轮数、记忆条数、工具调用次数、活跃时段），一个命令看清全貌

你觉得哪些有价值？我推荐 `/self`、`/stats`、`/sessions` 这三个最实用。

| 命令 | 功能 | 数据源 |

| `/self` | 自我画像 — 身份、身体、心智、历史、感知、记忆窗口 | SelfImage 运行时对象 |

**[23:53:39] 🟥用户**

现在都命令都分别在哪些文件里

---

**[23:53:51] 🤖助手**

命令分布在两个文件：

---

**`agent/commands.py`** — `MemoryConsole`，数据查看类，通过 `_DATA_CMDS` 路由

```
/user <名字>        切换用户身份
/db                 数据库大小/表/行数
/memory             最近长期记忆
/self               当前自我画像
/essence            底色（性格基线）
/stream [N]         最近经验流
/projects           项目心智模型
/clear              清空当前会话上下文
/new                新建会话
/context            查看完整上下文
/summarize          手动触发DAG压缩
/dag <关键词>       搜索DAG摘要
/expand <关键词>    展开DAG摘要原文
/periodic           手动触发定时记忆提取
/dream              手动触发梦境深度提取
/user-memories      用户记忆分布
/relationship       当前用户的关系数据
/learn              学习情况（队列 + 已学程序）
```

**`consciousness/living_commands.py`** — `COMMAND_REGISTRY`，系统/感官类，通过 `intent_cmds` 路由

```
/intent             当前意图
/fuel               手动触发加柴（L2）
/flame              火焰状态
/tick               心跳计数
/think              内在想法
/identity           意识全景 + /identity map
/drive              Drive 边缘系统
/purpose            Purpose 目标树
/plan               当前计划
/model              切换模型
/tool               展开工具调用详情
/export             导出会话 Markdown
/pace-stats         PACE 运行统计
/sessions           会话列表
/switch <session>   切换会话（数据命令用 /user；系统命令里也有 /user 切换身份 + SelfImage）
/user [id]          查看/切换身份（同时更新 SelfImage）
/eyes               眼睛状态
/ears               耳朵状态
/see                看当前场景
/hear               听周围声音
```

路由逻辑在 `gateway/inbound.py:224-281` 的 `_dispatch_command()`：
1. `_DATA_CMDS` 中的 → `MemoryConsole.execute()`
2. `/intask` `/inchat` → `ConversationDriver`
3. `COMMAND_REGISTRY` 中的 → 直接调用对应函数
4. 都不匹配 → 作为普通消息入队
